<td style="width: 0"></td><td style="width: 1in"><b>Item 5.02</b></td><td><b>Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements
of Certain Officers. </b></td></tr></table>

<p style="font: 10pt/120% Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in">On January 14, 2020, Ronald W. Allen
provided notice to The Coca-Cola Company (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) of his intention not to stand for reelection at the
Company&#8217;s 2020 Annual Meeting of Shareowners (the &#8220;2020 Annual Meeting&#8221;). Mr. Allen will remain a director
and maintain his committee memberships through the 2020 Annual Meeting.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.5in">A copy of the Company&#8217;s press release
is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and incorporated herein by reference.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt/normal Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&#160;</p>

<TEXT>
<HTML>
<HEAD>
     <TITLE></TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="text-align: right; margin: 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 12pt"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 54pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; letter-spacing: -5pt"><IMG SRC="image_002.jpg" ALT="" STYLE="height: 146px; width: 624px"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><B>The Coca-Cola Company Announces Retirement
of Ronald W. Allen </B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><B>from Board of Directors</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>ATLANTA, Jan. 14, 2020</B> &ndash; The Coca-Cola Company today
announced that Ronald W. Allen, 78, will not stand for reelection to the board of directors in April.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">Allen has been a director of the company since 1991. During his tenure
on the board, he has served on several committees and currently serves as chair of the audit committee.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">Allen&rsquo;s extensive leadership background includes 34 years at
Delta Air Lines, where he became president and chief operating officer in 1983. He was promoted to chairman and CEO in August 1987
and continued in that role until his retirement in August 1997. Allen led Delta&rsquo;s international expansion, including developing
Atlanta as a major international hub. With the acquisition of Pan American&rsquo;s European routes in 1991, Delta became the #1
airline between the United States and Europe.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">Allen also served as chairman and CEO of Aaron&rsquo;s Inc. during
a period of transition for the company from 2012 to 2014. He led the acquisition of Progressive Finance Holdings in 2014. He served
as a director of Aaron&rsquo;s from 1997 until 2014. He currently serves as a director of Forward&nbsp;Air Corp. and Aircastle
Limited.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&ldquo;It has been an honor to serve as a director of Coca-Cola for
29 years and to work with six different CEOs, beginning with Roberto Goizueta and ending with James Quincey,&rdquo; Allen said.
&ldquo;I am very confident of the continued success of The Coca-Cola Company under the leadership of James and his outstanding
leadership team.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&ldquo;Ron Allen has had a distinguished career, and we thank him
for his nearly three decades of service to The Coca-Cola Company,&rdquo; said Chairman and CEO James Quincey.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B><U>About The Coca-Cola Company</U></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">The Coca-Cola Company (NYSE: KO) is a total beverage company,
offering over 500 brands in more than 200 countries and territories. In addition to the company&rsquo;s Coca-Cola brand, our
portfolio includes AdeS, Ayataka, Costa, Dasani, Del Valle, Fanta, Georgia, Gold Peak, Honest, innocent, Minute Maid,
Powerade, Simply, smartwater, Sprite, vitaminwater and ZICO. We&rsquo;re constantly transforming our portfolio, from reducing
sugar in our drinks to bringing innovative new products to market. We&rsquo;re also working to reduce our environmental
impact by replenishing water and promoting recycling. With our bottling partners, we employ more than 700,000 people, helping
bring economic opportunity to local communities worldwide.&nbsp;Learn more at www.coca-colacompany.com and follow us on
Twitter, Instagram, Facebook and LinkedIn.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><B>Contacts:</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><U>Investors and Analysts:</U> Tim Leveridge, koinvestorrelations@coca-cola.com</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0"><U>Media:</U> Scott Leith, sleith@coca-cola.com</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Cambria, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>



<P STYLE="margin: 0"></P>
